                                second_pass_evidence_count += 1

                                # Also add to facts
                                all_facts.append({
                                    "text": fact.fact_text,
                                    "type": fact.fact_type,
                                    "confidence": fact.confidence,
                                    "source": source_analysis.source_url,
                                    "extraction_pass": 2,
                                })

                        # FIX 97 GHOST WIRING FIX: Second pass atomic facts
                        for atomic_fact in source_analysis.atomic_facts:
                            if not atomic_fact.statement or not atomic_fact.direct_quote:
                                continue

                            # FIX 111: Apply metadata filter to second pass too
                            FIX_111_METADATA_PATTERNS = [
                                r"^Document\s+(is|was|uses|contains|has|identifier)",
                                r"(PDF|file|format)\s+(structure|identifier|version|type)",
                                r"hosted\s+on\s+.*\s+domain",
                                r"accessible\s+through",
                                r"^(PURL|identifier|reference\s+number)",
                                r"(corrupted|not\s+readable|failed\s+to\s+parse)",
                                r"^\d+\s+objects?\s+in\s+PDF",
                                r"^Document\s+contains\s+\d+\s+(pages?|objects?)",
                                r"^(National\s+Service\s+Center|NSCEP)",
                                r"^(epa\.gov|nepis\.epa\.gov)\s+domain",
                            ]

                            # FIX-135A: PDF noise CONTENT patterns (second pass)
                            FIX_135_PDF_NOISE_PATTERNS = [
                                r"%PDF-\d",
                                r"corrupted\s+or\s+binary\s+encoded",
                                r"preventing\s+text\s+extraction",
                                r"binary\s+encoded\s+content",
                                r"PDF\s+document\s+(could\s+not|cannot|failed\s+to)",
                                r"text\s+extraction\s+(was\s+not|is\s+not)\s+possible",
                                r"garbled\s+(text|content|output)",
                                r"encoding\s+(error|issue|problem).*PDF",
                                r"unreadable\s+(due\s+to|because)",
                                r"document\s+appears\s+to\s+be\s+(corrupt|damaged|binary)",
                                # FIX-142: Additional PDF noise patterns from gap analysis
                                r"not\s+directly\s+extractable",
                                r"minimal\s+extractable",
                                r"\bcorrupted\b(?!\s+or\s+binary)",
                                r"PDF-\d+\.\d+",
                            ]

                            is_metadata_garbage = any(
                                re.search(pattern, atomic_fact.direct_quote, re.IGNORECASE)
                                for pattern in FIX_111_METADATA_PATTERNS
                            )

                            is_pdf_noise = any(
                                re.search(pattern, atomic_fact.direct_quote, re.IGNORECASE)
                                for pattern in FIX_135_PDF_NOISE_PATTERNS
                            )

                            if is_metadata_garbage:
                                logger.warning(
                                    f"[FIX 111 P2] Filtering metadata evidence: "
                                    f"{atomic_fact.direct_quote[:60]}..."
                                )
                                continue

                            if is_pdf_noise:
                                logger.warning(
                                    f"[FIX-135 P2] Filtering PDF noise content: "
                                    f"{atomic_fact.direct_quote[:60]}..."
                                )
                                continue

                            content_hash = hashlib.md5(
                                atomic_fact.direct_quote.strip().lower().encode()
                            ).hexdigest()

                            if content_hash not in seen_content_hashes and len(all_evidence) < evidence_cap:
                                seen_content_hashes.add(content_hash)

                                atomic_ev_id = f"ev_atomic_{hashlib.md5((source_analysis.source_url + 
atomic_fact.statement).encode()).hexdigest()[:12]}_p2"
                                atomic_chunk_id = 
f"chunk_atomic_{hashlib.md5(source_analysis.source_url.encode()).hexdigest()[:8]}_p2"

                                # FIX 113: Evidence Text Enrichment - Include context
                                enriched_text = f"{atomic_fact.statement}. Source quote: 
\"{atomic_fact.direct_quote}\""

                                atomic_evidence = Evidence(
                                    evidence_id=atomic_ev_id,
                                    chunk_id=atomic_chunk_id,
                                    source_url=source_analysis.source_url,
                                    title=url_to_title_p2.get(source_analysis.source_url, ""),  # FIX-180A
                                    text=enriched_text[:2000],  # FIX 113: Use enriched text
                                    relevance_score=min(1.0, source_analysis.relevance_score + 0.15),  # Higher boost 
for pass 2
                                    source_quality_score=source_analysis.source_quality,
                                    extraction_method="atomic_fact_extraction_pass_2",
                                    claims=[atomic_fact.statement],
                                    entities=atomic_fact.entities,
                                    quality_tier="GOLD",  # Pass 2 atomic = GOLD
                                    is_metadata=False,
                                    atomic_facts=[atomic_fact],
                                    perspective_origins=p2_perspectives,  # FIX-124: STORM traceability
                                    authors=url_to_authors_p2.get(source_analysis.source_url, []),  # FIX-227
                                )
                                all_evidence.append(atomic_evidence)
                                second_pass_evidence_count += 1
                                logger.info(
                                    f"[FIX 97 P2] Atomic evidence {atomic_ev_id}: "
                                    f"{atomic_fact.fact_category} - {atomic_fact.statement[:40]}..."
                                )

                logger.info(
                    f"[W3.1 MULTI-PASS] Second pass complete: {second_pass_evidence_count} "
                    f"new evidence pieces from {len(high_quality_sources)} sources"
                )
                state["multi_pass_stats"] = {
                    "enabled": True,
                    "high_quality_sources": len(high_quality_sources),
                    "second_pass_evidence": second_pass_evidence_count,
                }
            else:
                logger.info("[W3.1 MULTI-PASS] No high-quality sources found for second pass")
                state["multi_pass_stats"] = {
                    "enabled": True,
                    "high_quality_sources": 0,
                    "second_pass_evidence": 0,
                }

        # Update state
        state["evidence_chain"] = all_evidence
        state["entities_extracted"] = all_entities
        state["facts_extracted"] = all_facts

        # ======================================================================
        # FIX-137A: Retroactive Perspective Tagging
        # ======================================================================
        # STORM perspective_origins is only populated for perspective-specific
        # query results. General web search results (85% of evidence) have no
        # tags, making entropy calculation unrepresentative. This step assigns
        # perspectives to untagged evidence via keyword matching.
        self._retroactive_perspective_tag(all_evidence)

        # SOTA FIX: Log quality tier distribution
        tier_counts = {"GOLD": 0, "SILVER": 0, "BRONZE": 0, "UNVERIFIED": 0}
        for ev in all_evidence:
            tier_counts[ev.quality_tier] = tier_counts.get(ev.quality_tier, 0) + 1

        logger.info(
            f"Analysis complete: {len(all_evidence)} evidence pieces, "
            f"{len(all_entities)} entities, {len(all_facts)} facts"
        )
        logger.info(
            f"Quality tier distribution: GOLD={tier_counts['GOLD']}, "
            f"SILVER={tier_counts['SILVER']}, BRONZE={tier_counts['BRONZE']}, "
            f"UNVERIFIED={tier_counts['UNVERIFIED']}"
        )
        logger.info(
            f"Deduplication: {duplicate_count} duplicates filtered, "
            f"{len(seen_content_hashes)} unique content hashes"
        )
        state["quality_tier_distribution"] = tier_counts
        state["duplicate_count"] = duplicate_count

        # ======================================================================
        # SOTA Integration: Advanced Deduplication (Task #21)
        # ======================================================================
        try:
            if all_evidence and len(all_evidence) > 1:
                dedup = ContentDeduplicator()
                # Convert evidence to format expected by deduplicator
                evidence_texts = []
                for ev in all_evidence:
                    ev_dict = ev.model_dump() if hasattr(ev, "model_dump") else ev if isinstance(ev, dict) else {}
                    evidence_texts.append({
                        "id": ev_dict.get("evidence_id", ""),
                        "content": ev_dict.get("text", ""),
                        "metadata": ev_dict,
                    })

                dedup_result = dedup.deduplicate(evidence_texts)
                state["advanced_dedup_stats"] = {
                    "original_count": len(all_evidence),
                    "unique_count": dedup_result.unique_count,
                    "duplicate_count": dedup_result.duplicate_count,
                    "deduplication_ratio": dedup_result.deduplication_ratio,
                }
                logger.info(
                    f"[DEDUP] Advanced deduplication: {len(all_evidence)} -> {dedup_result.unique_count} "
                    f"({dedup_result.deduplication_ratio*100:.1f}% reduction)"
                )
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"[DEDUP] Advanced deduplication failed: {e}")

        # ======================================================================
        # SOTA Integration: Source Bias Detection (Task #21)
        # ======================================================================
        try:
            if all_evidence:
                bias_detector = BiasDetector()
                # Convert evidence to format expected by bias detector
                evidence_for_bias = []
                for ev in all_evidence:
                    ev_dict = ev.model_dump() if hasattr(ev, "model_dump") else ev if isinstance(ev, dict) else {}
                    evidence_for_bias.append({
                        "source_url": ev_dict.get("source_url", ""),
                        "text": ev_dict.get("text", ""),
                        "title": ev_dict.get("title", ""),
                    })

                bias_report = bias_detector.analyze_sources(evidence_for_bias)
                state["bias_analysis"] = {
                    "is_balanced": bias_report.is_balanced,
                    "balance_score": bias_report.balance_score,
                    "category_distribution": {
                        cat.value: count for cat, count in bias_report.category_distribution.items()
                    },
                    "balance_warning": bias_report.balance_warning,
                    "suggestions": bias_report.balancing_suggestions,
                }
                if not bias_report.is_balanced:
                    logger.warning(f"[BIAS] Unbalanced sources detected: {bias_report.balance_warning}")
                else:
                    logger.info(f"[BIAS] Sources balanced: score={bias_report.balance_score:.2f}")
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"[BIAS] Bias detection failed: {e}")

        # Enrich with knowledge graph
        state = self._enrich_with_graph(state, all_entities, all_facts)

        return state

    def _retroactive_perspective_tag(self, evidence_list: List[Evidence]) -> None:
        """
        FIX-137A: Assign perspectives to untagged evidence via keyword matching.

        STORM perspective_origins is only populated for perspective-specific query
        results. General web search results (~85% of evidence) have no tags.
        This retroactive tagging improves entropy calculation representativeness.

        Rules:
        - Does NOT override existing STORM tags
        - Marks tagged items with perspective_source="retroactive_keyword" for provenance
        - Modifies evidence objects in-place
        """
        perspective_keywords = {
            "Scientific": [
                "study", "research", "findings", "experiment", "data",
                "analysis", "evidence", "methodology", "peer-reviewed",
                "published", "journal", "laboratory", "clinical",
            ],
            "Regulatory": [
                "regulation", "compliance", "epa", "fda", "standard",
                "guideline", "policy", "enforcement", "mandate", "act",
                "law", "requirement", "permitted", "threshold",
            ],
            "Public_Health": [
                "health", "disease", "risk", "exposure", "epidemiology",
                "mortality", "morbidity", "outbreak", "contamination",
                "toxicity", "carcinogen", "safety", "wellbeing",
            ],
            "Economic": [
                "cost", "price", "market", "economic", "investment",
                "savings", "budget", "affordable", "expense", "revenue",
                "[7mfinancial", "trade", "industry revenue[0m",[0m
[7m[0m            ],[0m
[7m[0m            "Industry": [[0m
[7m[0m                "manufacturer", "product", "commercial", "brand",[0m
[7m[0m                "technology", "innovation", "patent", "production",[0m
[7m[0m                "supply chain", "vendor", "certification",[0m
[7m[0m            ],[0m
[7m[0m            "Regional": [[0m
[7m[0m                "local", "regional", "community", "municipal", "rural",[0m
[7m[0m                "urban", "geographic", "county", "district", "state-level",[0m
[7m[0m            ],[0m
[7m[0m            "Historical": [[0m
[7m[0m                "history", "historical", "decade", "century", "evolution",[0m
[7m[0m                "timeline", "previously", "originally", "legacy",[0m
[7m[0m            ],[0m
[7m[0m            "Emerging_Trends": [[0m
[7m[0m                "emerging", "novel", "recent", "trend", "future",[0m
[7m[0m                "advancing", "next-generation", "cutting-edge", "latest",[0m
[7m[0m            ],[0m
[7m[0m        }[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        tagged_count = 0[0m
[7m[0m        for ev in evidence_list:[0m
[7m[0m            # Access perspective_origins (handle both Pydantic and dict)[0m
[7m[0m            if hasattr(ev, "perspective_origins"):[0m
[7m[0m                existing = ev.perspective_origins or [][0m
[7m[0m            elif isinstance(ev, dict):[0m
[7m[0m                existing = ev.get("perspective_origins", [])[0m
[7m[0m            else:[0m
[7m[0m                continue[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # Skip if already tagged by STORM[0m
[7m[0m            if existing:[0m
[7m[0m                continue[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # Get evidence text for keyword matching[0m
[7m[0m            if hasattr(ev, "text"):[0m
[7m[0m                text = (ev.text or "").lower()[0m
[7m[0m            elif isinstance(ev, dict):[0m
[7m[0m                text = (ev.get("text", "") or "").lower()[0m
[7m[0m            else:[0m
[7m[0m                continue[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            if not text:[0m
[7m[0m                continue[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # FIX-165: Get source URL for domain-based tagging[0m
[7m[0m            if hasattr(ev, "source_url"):[0m
[7m[0m                source_url = (ev.source_url or "").lower()[0m
[7m[0m            elif isinstance(ev, dict):[0m
[7m[0m                source_url = (ev.get("source_url", "") or "").lower()[0m
[7m[0m            else:[0m
[7m[0m                source_url = ""[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # Score each perspective by keyword hits[0m
[7m[0m            # FIX-165: Case-insensitive substring matching (already lowercase)[0m
[7m[0m            best_perspective = None[0m
[7m[0m            best_score = 0[0m
[7m[0m            for perspective, keywords in perspective_keywords.items():[0m
[7m[0m                score = sum(1 for kw in keywords if kw in text)[0m
[7m[0m                if score > best_score:[0m
[7m[0m                    best_score = score[0m
[7m[0m                    best_perspective = perspective[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # FIX-165: Domain-based tagging fallback[0m
[7m[0m            if best_score < 1 and source_url:[0m
[7m[0m                domain_perspective_map = {[0m
[7m[0m                    ".edu": "Scientific",[0m
[7m[0m                    ".gov": "Regulatory",[0m
[7m[0m                    "pubmed": "Scientific",[0m
[7m[0m                    "scholar.google": "Scientific",[0m
[7m[0m                    "ncbi.nlm.nih": "Scientific",[0m
[7m[0m                    "who.int": "Public_Health",[0m
[7m[0m                    "cdc.gov": "Public_Health",[0m
[7m[0m                    "epa.gov": "Regulatory",[0m
[7m[0m                    "fda.gov": "Regulatory",[0m
[7m[0m                }[0m
[7m[0m                for domain_key, perspective in domain_perspective_map.items():[0m
[7m[0m                    if domain_key in source_url:[0m
[7m[0m                        best_perspective = perspective[0m
[7m[0m                        best_score = 1  # Domain match counts as 1 hit[0m
[7m[0m                        break[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # FIX-165: Lowered threshold from 2 to 1 keyword hit[0m
[7m[0m            if best_perspective and best_score >= 1:[0m
[7m[0m                if hasattr(ev, "perspective_origins"):[0m
[7m[0m                    ev.perspective_origins = [best_perspective][0m
[7m[0m                    ev.perspective_source = "retroactive_keyword"[0m
[7m[0m                elif isinstance(ev, dict):[0m
[7m[0m                    ev["perspective_origins"] = [best_perspective][0m
[7m[0m                    ev["perspective_source"] = "retroactive_keyword"[0m
[7m[0m                tagged_count += 1[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        total = len(evidence_list)[0m
[7m[0m        if tagged_count > 0:[0m
[7m[0m            logger.info([0m
[7m[0m                f"[FIX-165] Retroactive perspective tagging: "[0m
[7m[0m                f"{tagged_count}/{total} evidence items tagged "[0m
[7m[0m                f"({tagged_count/max(total,1)*100:.0f}%)"[0m
[7m[0m            )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    def _enrich_with_graph([0m
[7m[0m        self,[0m
[7m[0m        state: ResearchState,[0m
[7m[0m        entities: List[Dict[str, Any]],[0m
[7m[0m        facts: List[Dict[str, Any]][0m
[7m[0m    ) -> ResearchState:[0m
[7m[0m        """[0m
[7m[0m        Enrich entities and facts with knowledge graph.[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        - Add extracted entities to the graph[0m
[7m[0m        - Retrieve related entities for context expansion[0m
[7m[0m        - Find relationships between extracted entities[0m
[7m[0m        """[0m
[7m[0m        try:[0m
[7m[0m            from src.graph import ([0m
[7m[0m                get_graph_client,[0m
[7m[0m                extract_entities as graph_extract_entities,[0m
[7m[0m                extract_relationships,[0m
[7m[0m                add_entities_to_graph,[0m
[7m[0m                add_relationships_to_graph,[0m
[7m[0m                get_graph_retriever,[0m
[7m[0m                expand_context,[0m
[7m[0m            )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            client = get_graph_client()[0m
[7m[0m            retriever = get_graph_retriever()[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # Track graph enrichment results[0m
[7m[0m            graph_enrichment = {[0m
[7m[0m                "entities_added": 0,[0m
[7m[0m                "relationships_added": 0,[0m
[7m[0m                "context_expansions": [],[0m
[7m[0m            }[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # Add entities to graph for each fact[0m
[7m[0m            for fact in facts:[0m
[7m[0m                fact_text = fact.get("text", "")[0m
[7m[0m                source_url = fact.get("source", "")[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                if not fact_text:[0m
[7m[0m                    continue[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                # Generate chunk ID from fact[0m
[7m[0m                chunk_id = hashlib.md5(fact_text.encode()).hexdigest()[:12][0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                # Extract entities from fact text[0m
[7m[0m                extraction_result = graph_extract_entities([0m
[7m[0m                    text=fact_text,[0m
[7m[0m                    chunk_id=chunk_id,[0m
[7m[0m                    source_url=source_url,[0m
[7m[0m                    use_llm=False  # Use patterns only for speed[0m
[7m[0m                )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                # Add to graph[0m
[7m[0m                if extraction_result.entities:[0m
[7m[0m                    count = add_entities_to_graph(extraction_result, client)[0m
[7m[0m                    graph_enrichment["entities_added"] += count[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                    # Extract relationships[0m
[7m[0m                    rel_result = extract_relationships([0m
[7m[0m                        text=fact_text,[0m
[7m[0m                        entities=extraction_result.entities,[0m
[7m[0m                        chunk_id=chunk_id,[0m
[7m[0m                        source_url=source_url,[0m
[7m[0m                        use_llm=False[0m
[7m[0m                    )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                    if rel_result.relationships:[0m
[7m[0m                        rel_count = add_relationships_to_graph([0m
[7m[0m                            rel_result,[0m
[7m[0m                            extraction_result,[0m
[7m[0m                            client[0m
[7m[0m                        )[0m
[7m[0m                        graph_enrichment["relationships_added"] += rel_count[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # Expand context for key entities[0m
[7m[0m            for entity in entities[:10]:  # Top 10 entities[0m
[7m[0m                entity_text = entity.get("text", "")[0m
[7m[0m                if not entity_text:[0m
[7m[0m                    continue[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                # Search for matching entity in graph[0m
[7m[0m                nodes = client.search_nodes(query=entity_text, limit=1)[0m
[7m[0m                if nodes:[0m
[7m[0m                    # Expand context around this entity[0m
[7m[0m                    expansion = expand_context([0m
[7m[0m                        entity_id=nodes[0].entity_id,[0m
[7m[0m                        graph_retriever=retriever,[0m
[7m[0m                        depth=1,[0m
[7m[0m                        max_neighbors=5[0m
[7m[0m                    )[0m
[7m[0m                    if expansion.get("total_entities", 0) > 1:[0m
[7m[0m                        graph_enrichment["context_expansions"].append({[0m
[7m[0m                            "entity": entity_text,[0m
[7m[0m                            "neighbors": expansion.get("total_entities", 0),[0m
[7m[0m                            "relationships": expansion.get("total_relationships", 0),[0m
[7m[0m                        })[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # Store enrichment results in state[0m
[7m[0m            state["graph_enrichment"] = graph_enrichment[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            logger.info([0m
[7m[0m                f"Graph enrichment: {graph_enrichment['entities_added']} entities, "[0m
[7m[0m                f"{graph_enrichment['relationships_added']} relationships, "[0m
[7m[0m                f"{len(graph_enrichment['context_expansions'])} expansions"[0m
[7m[0m            )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        except ImportError as e:[0m
[7m[0m            logger.warning(f"Graph module not available for enrichment: {e}")[0m
[7m[0m        except Exception as e:[0m
[7m[0m            logger.error(f"Graph enrichment failed: {e}")[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        return state[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    def _fetch_content(self, search_results: List[SearchResult]) -> List[SearchResult]:[0m
[7m[0m        """[0m
[7m[0m        Fetch full content for search results that need it.[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        P2.5 GAP FIX: Uses context manager for proper socket cleanup.[0m
[7m[0m        """[0m
[7m[0m        import requests[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        # Get configurable content limit (LAW VI)[0m
[7m[0m        max_content = self.depth_config.evidence_extraction.max_fetch_content[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        # P2.5 GAP FIX: Use session with context manager for proper socket cleanup[0m
[7m[0m        # FIX 100: Add progress logging for content fetch phase[0m
[7m[0m        total_to_fetch = len(search_results)[0m
[7m[0m        fetched_count = 0[0m
[7m[0m        success_count = 0[0m
[7m[0m        logger.info(f"[CONTENT-FETCH] Starting content fetch for {total_to_fetch} URLs")[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        with requests.Session() as session:[0m
[7m[0m            session.headers.update({[0m
[7m[0m                "User-Agent": "POLARIS Research Bot/1.0"[0m
[7m[0m            })[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            for idx, result in enumerate(search_results):[0m
[7m[0m                if result.content:[0m
[7m[0m                    fetched_count += 1[0m
[7m[0m                    success_count += 1[0m
[7m[0m                    continue  # Already has content[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                if result.fetch_status == "failed":[0m
[7m[0m                    fetched_count += 1[0m
[7m[0m                    continue  # Don't retry failed fetches[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                try:[0m
[7m[0m                    # P2.5: Session automatically manages connection pooling and cleanup[0m
[7m[0m                    response = session.get(result.url, timeout=10)[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                    if response.status_code == 200:[0m
[7m[0m                        # Extract text content with configurable limit[0m
[7m[0m                        content = self._extract_text(response.text)[0m
[7m[0m                        result.content = content[:max_content][0m
[7m[0m                        result.fetch_status = "success"[0m
[7m[0m                        success_count += 1[0m
[7m[0m                    else:[0m
[7m[0m                        result.fetch_status = "failed"[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                except Exception as e:[0m
[7m[0m                    logger.warning(f"Failed to fetch {result.url}: {e}")[0m
[7m[0m                    result.fetch_status = "failed"[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                fetched_count += 1[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                # FIX 100: Log progress every 20 URLs[0m
[7m[0m                if fetched_count % 20 == 0:[0m
[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m [0m[7m[0mlogger.info(f"[CONTENT-FETCH] [0m[7m[0mProgress: [0m[7m[0m{fetched_count}/{total_to_fetch} [0m[7m[0mURLs [0m[7m[0m({success_count} [0m
[7m[0msuccess)")[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        logger.info(f"[CONTENT-FETCH] Complete: {success_count}/{total_to_fetch} URLs fetched successfully")[0m
[7m[0m        # Session is automatically closed here, all sockets cleaned up[0m
[7m[0m        return search_results[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    def _extract_text(self, html: str) -> str:[0m
[7m[0m        """Extract text content from HTML."""[0m
[7m[0m        try:[0m
[7m[0m            from bs4 import BeautifulSoup[0m
[7m[0m            soup = BeautifulSoup(html, "html.parser")[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # Remove script and style elements[0m
[7m[0m            for script in soup(["script", "style", "nav", "footer", "header"]):[0m
[7m[0m                script.decompose()[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # Get text[0m
[7m[0m            text = soup.get_text(separator="\n")[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # Clean up[0m
[7m[0m            lines = (line.strip() for line in text.splitlines())[0m
[7m[0m            chunks = (phrase.strip() for line in lines for phrase in line.split("  "))[0m
[7m[0m            text = "\n".join(chunk for chunk in chunks if chunk)[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            return text[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        except ImportError:[0m
[7m[0m            # Fallback: simple regex extraction[0m
[7m[0m            import re[0m
[7m[0m            text = re.sub(r"<[^>]+>", " ", html)[0m
[7m[0m            text = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", text)[0m
[7m[0m            return text.strip()[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    def _analyze_batch([0m
[7m[0m        self,[0m
[7m[0m        batch: List[SearchResult],[0m
[7m[0m        original_query: str,[0m
[7m[0m        state: ResearchState[0m
[7m[0m    ) -> AnalysisOutput:[0m
[7m[0m        """Analyze a batch of search results with SOTA-level depth."""[0m
[7m[0m        # Get configurable limits (LAW VI)[0m
[7m[0m        content_limit = self.depth_config.evidence_extraction.content_chunk_size[0m
[7m[0m        max_claims = self.depth_config.evidence_extraction.max_claims[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        # P3.1 GAP FIX: Get extraction limits from extraction.yaml config[0m
[7m[0m        extraction_cfg = _EXTRACTION_CONFIG.get("extraction", {})[0m
[7m[0m        entities_per_source = extraction_cfg.get("entities_per_source", 5)[0m
[7m[0m        facts_per_source = extraction_cfg.get("facts_per_source", 10)[0m
[7m[0m        claims_per_source = extraction_cfg.get("claims_per_source", 5)[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        logger.debug([0m
[7m[0m            f"[P3.1] Using extraction limits: entities={entities_per_source}, "[0m
[7m[0m            f"facts={facts_per_source}, claims={claims_per_source}"[0m
[7m[0m        )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        # Build content for analysis[0m
[7m[0m        source_contents = [][0m
[7m[0m        for result in batch:[0m
[7m[0m            content = result.content or result.snippet[0m
[7m[0m            if not content:[0m
[7m[0m                continue[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            source_contents.append(f"""[0m
[7m[0mSOURCE: {result.url}[0m
[7m[0mTITLE: {result.title}[0m
[7m[0mTYPE: {result.source_type}[0m
[7m[0mDOMAIN: {result.domain}[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0mCONTENT:[0m
[7m[0m{content[:content_limit]}[0m
[7m[0m""")[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        if not source_contents:[0m
[7m[0m            return AnalysisOutput([0m
[7m[0m                analyses=[],[0m
[7m[0m                cross_source_entities=[],[0m
[7m[0m                contradictions=[],[0m
[7m[0m                evidence_summary="No content available for analysis"[0m
[7m[0m            )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        sources_text = "\n---\n".join(source_contents)[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        # P3.1 GAP FIX: Use config values in prompt instead of hardcoded values[0m
[7m[0m        messages = [[0m
[7m[0m            SystemMessage(content=self.get_system_prompt()),[0m
[7m[0m            HumanMessage(content=f"""Analyze these sources for the research question.[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0mRESEARCH QUESTION: {original_query}[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0mAPPLICATION: {state.get('application', 'Unknown')}[0m
[7m[0mREGION: {state.get('region', 'GLOBAL')}[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0mSOURCES:[0m
[7m[0m{sources_text}[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0mEXTRACTION REQUIREMENTS:[0m
[7m[0m- [0m[7m[0mExtract [0m[7m[0mup [0m[7m[0mto [0m[7m[0m{entities_per_source} [0m[7m[0mnamed [0m[7m[0mentities [0m[7m[0mper [0m[7m[0msource [0m[7m[0m(people, [0m[7m[0morganizations, [0m[7m[0mchemicals, [0m[7m[0mmeasurements, [0m
[7m[0mregulations)[0m
[7m[0m- Extract up to {facts_per_source} factual statements per source with supporting text[0m
[7m[0m- Extract up to {claims_per_source} verifiable claims per source[0m
[7m[0m- Target {max_claims} total claims across all sources[0m
[7m[0m- Provide source quality assessment (0.0-1.0 scale)[0m
[7m[0m- Assess relevance to research question (0.0-1.0 scale)[0m
[7m[0m- Identify contradictions between sources[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0mFocus on the most relevant and verifiable evidence.""")[0m
[7m[0m        ][0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        try:[0m
[7m[0m            analysis: AnalysisOutput = self.call_llm_structured(messages, AnalysisOutput)[0m
[7m[0m            # FIX 12: Handle None return from call_llm_structured (timeout or parse failure)[0m
[7m[0m            # Without this check, the caller crashes on analysis.analyses when analysis is None[0m
[7m[0m            if analysis is None:[0m
[7m[0m                logger.warning("LLM returned None for batch analysis (timeout or parsing failure), skipping batch")[0m
[7m[0m                return AnalysisOutput([0m
[7m[0m                    analyses=[],[0m
[7m[0m                    cross_source_entities=[],[0m
[7m[0m                    contradictions=[],[0m
[7m[0m                    evidence_summary="Analysis timed out or failed to parse"[0m
[7m[0m                )[0m
[7m[0m            return analysis[0m
[7m[0m        except Exception as e:[0m
[7m[0m            logger.error(f"Analysis failed: {e}")[0m
[7m[0m            return AnalysisOutput([0m
[7m[0m                analyses=[],[0m
[7m[0m                cross_source_entities=[],[0m
[7m[0m                contradictions=[],[0m
[7m[0m                evidence_summary=f"Analysis failed: {str(e)}"[0m
[7m[0m            )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    def _analyze_batch_deep([0m
[7m[0m        self,[0m
[7m[0m        batch: List[SearchResult],[0m
[7m[0m        original_query: str,[0m
[7m[0m        state: ResearchState,[0m
[7m[0m        first_pass_results: List[dict][0m
[7m[0m    ) -> AnalysisOutput:[0m
[7m[0m        """[0m
[7m[0m        W3.1 SOTA: Second-pass deep extraction for high-quality sources.[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        This method performs deeper analysis focusing on:[0m
[7m[0m        - Supporting evidence for existing claims[0m
[7m[0m        - Counterarguments and contradicting evidence[0m
[7m[0m        - Relationships between entities[0m
[7m[0m        - Statistical data and measurements[0m
[7m[0m        - Methodology and limitations[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        Only called for sources that meet the quality threshold.[0m
[7m[0m        """[0m
[7m[0m        if not _MULTI_PASS_CONFIG.get("enabled", True):[0m
[7m[0m            # Return empty if multi-pass disabled[0m
[7m[0m            return AnalysisOutput([0m
[7m[0m                analyses=[],[0m
[7m[0m                cross_source_entities=[],[0m
[7m[0m                contradictions=[],[0m
[7m[0m                evidence_summary="Multi-pass disabled"[0m
[7m[0m            )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        content_limit = self.depth_config.evidence_extraction.content_chunk_size[0m
[7m[0m        evidence_per_pass = _MULTI_PASS_CONFIG.get("evidence_per_pass", 15)[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        # Build content for deep analysis[0m
[7m[0m        source_contents = [][0m
[7m[0m        for result in batch:[0m
[7m[0m            content = result.content or result.snippet[0m
[7m[0m            if not content:[0m
[7m[0m                continue[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            source_contents.append(f"""[0m
[7m[0mSOURCE: {result.url}[0m
[7m[0mTITLE: {result.title}[0m
[7m[0mTYPE: {result.source_type}[0m
[7m[0mDOMAIN: {result.domain}[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0mCONTENT:[0m
[7m[0m{content[:content_limit]}[0m
[7m[0m""")[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        if not source_contents:[0m
[7m[0m            return AnalysisOutput([0m
[7m[0m                analyses=[],[0m
[7m[0m                cross_source_entities=[],[0m
[7m[0m                contradictions=[],[0m
[7m[0m                evidence_summary="No content for deep analysis"[0m
[7m[0m            )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        sources_text = "\n---\n".join(source_contents)[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        # Build context from first pass results[0m
[7m[0m        first_pass_context = ""[0m
[7m[0m        if first_pass_results:[0m
[7m[0m            facts_summary = [r.get("text", "")[:100] for r in first_pass_results[:10]][0m
[7m[0m            first_pass_context = f"""[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0mFIRST PASS FINDINGS (for context):[0m
[7m[0m{chr(10).join(f'- {f}' for f in facts_summary if f)}[0m
[7m[0m"""[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        # Deep analysis prompt - focus on supporting evidence and relationships[0m
[7m[0m        messages = [[0m
[7m[0m            SystemMessage(content=self.get_system_prompt()),[0m
[7m[0m            HumanMessage(content=f"""Perform DEEP SECOND-PASS analysis on these sources.[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0mRESEARCH QUESTION: {original_query}[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0mAPPLICATION: {state.get('application', 'Unknown')}[0m
[7m[0mREGION: {state.get('region', 'GLOBAL')}[0m
[7m[0m{first_pass_context}[0m
[7m[0mSOURCES:[0m
[7m[0m{sources_text}[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0mSECOND-PASS EXTRACTION (Focus on what first pass might have missed):[0m
[7m[0m1. SUPPORTING EVIDENCE: Find specific data, statistics, or quotes that support the main claims[0m
[7m[0m2. COUNTERARGUMENTS: Identify any contradicting evidence, caveats, or limitations[0m
[7m[0m3. RELATIONSHIPS: Identify connections between entities (e.g., "X causes Y", "A regulates B")[0m
[7m[0m4. METHODOLOGY: Extract study design, sample sizes, confidence intervals if available[0m
[7m[0m5. CONTEXT: Historical context, geographic specifics, regulatory frameworks[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0mExtract up to {evidence_per_pass} deep evidence items per source.[0m
[7m[0mFocus on quantitative data, specific citations, and nuanced findings.""")[0m
[7m[0m        ][0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        try:[0m
[7m[0m            analysis: AnalysisOutput = self.call_llm_structured(messages, AnalysisOutput)[0m
[7m[0m            if analysis is None:[0m
[7m[0m                logger.warning("Deep analysis returned None, skipping")[0m
[7m[0m                return AnalysisOutput([0m
[7m[0m                    analyses=[],[0m
[7m[0m                    cross_source_entities=[],[0m
[7m[0m                    contradictions=[],[0m
[7m[0m                    evidence_summary="Deep analysis timed out"[0m
[7m[0m                )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            logger.info([0m
[7m[0m                f"[W3.1 MULTI-PASS] Second pass extracted "[0m
[7m[0m                f"{sum(len(a.facts) for a in analysis.analyses)} additional facts"[0m
[7m[0m            )[0m
[7m[0m            return analysis[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        except Exception as e:[0m
[7m[0m            logger.error(f"Deep analysis failed: {e}")[0m
[7m[0m            return AnalysisOutput([0m
[7m[0m                analyses=[],[0m
[7m[0m                cross_source_entities=[],[0m
[7m[0m                contradictions=[],[0m
[7m[0m                evidence_summary=f"Deep analysis failed: {str(e)}"[0m
[7m[0m            )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    def _analyze_multimodal([0m
[7m[0m        self,[0m
[7m[0m        search_results: List[SearchResult],[0m
[7m[0m        original_query: str[0m
[7m[0m    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:[0m
[7m[0m        """[0m
[7m[0m        Analyze multimodal content (PDFs, images) from search results.[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        Uses Gemini vision for image/chart analysis and PDF parsing[0m
[7m[0m        for document extraction.[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        Args:[0m
[7m[0m            search_results: Search results that may contain PDFs or images[0m
[7m[0m            original_query: Research question for context[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        Returns:[0m
[7m[0m            Dict with multimodal analysis results[0m
[7m[0m        """[0m
[7m[0m        multimodal_results = {[0m
[7m[0m            "pdf_analyses": [],[0m
[7m[0m            "image_analyses": [],[0m
[7m[0m            "extracted_data": [],[0m
[7m[0m        }[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        try:[0m
[7m[0m            from src.tools import ([0m
[7m[0m                get_vision_client,[0m
[7m[0m                get_pdf_parser,[0m
[7m[0m                analyze_research_image,[0m
[7m[0m                quick_pdf_extract,[0m
[7m[0m            )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m            # Identify multimodal content[0m
[7m[0m            for result in search_results:[0m
[7m[0m                url = result.url.lower()[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                # Check for PDFs[0m
[7m[0m                if url.endswith(".pdf"):[0m
[7m[0m                    try:[0m
[7m[0m                        # For remote PDFs, we'd need to download first[0m
[7m[0m                        # For now, log and skip remote PDFs[0m
[7m[0m                        if url.startswith("http"):[0m
[7m[0m                            logger.info(f"Skipping remote PDF: {result.url}")[0m
[7m[0m                            continue[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                        pdf_data = quick_pdf_extract(result.url)[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                        if "error" not in pdf_data:[0m
[7m[0m                            multimodal_results["pdf_analyses"].append({[0m
[7m[0m                                "url": result.url,[0m
[7m[0m                                "metadata": pdf_data.get("metadata", {}),[0m
[7m[0m                                "table_count": len(pdf_data.get("tables", [])),[0m
[7m[0m                                "text_preview": pdf_data.get("text", "")[:1000],[0m
[7m[0m                                "tables": pdf_data.get("tables", [])[:5],  # Limit tables[0m
[7m[0m                            })[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                            # Add tables as extracted data[0m
[7m[0m                            for table in pdf_data.get("tables", [])[:5]:[0m
[7m[0m                                multimodal_results["extracted_data"].append({[0m
[7m[0m                                    "type": "table",[0m
[7m[0m                                    "source": result.url,[0m
[7m[0m                                    "headers": table.get("headers", []),[0m
[7m[0m                                    "row_count": len(table.get("rows", [])),[0m
[7m[0m                                })[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                    except Exception as e:[0m
[7m[0m                        logger.warning(f"PDF analysis failed for {result.url}: {e}")[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                # Check for images[0m
[7m[0m                elif any(url.endswith(ext) for ext in [".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".gif", ".webp"]):[0m
[7m[0m                    try:[0m
[7m[0m                        # For remote images, we can pass URL to vision client[0m
[7m[0m                        if url.startswith("http"):[0m
[7m[0m                            image_data = analyze_research_image([0m
[7m[0m                                result.url,[0m
[7m[0m                                context=original_query[0m
[7m[0m                            )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                            if "error" not in image_data.get("general_analysis", {}):[0m
[7m[0m                                multimodal_results["image_analyses"].append({[0m
[7m[0m                                    "url": result.url,[0m
[7m[0m                                    "image_type": image_data.get("image_type", "other"),[0m
[7m[0m                                    "analysis": image_data.get("general_analysis", {}),[0m
[7m[0m                                    "chart_data": image_data.get("chart_data"),[0m
[7m[0m                                    "table_data": image_data.get("table_data"),[0m
[7m[0m                                })[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                                # Add chart/table data as extracted data[0m
[7m[0m                                if image_data.get("chart_data"):[0m
[7m[0m                                    multimodal_results["extracted_data"].append({[0m
[7m[0m                                        "type": "chart",[0m
[7m[0m                                        "source": result.url,[0m
[7m[0m                                        "chart_type": image_data["chart_data"].get("chart_type"),[0m
[7m[0m                                        "title": image_data["chart_data"].get("title"),[0m
[7m[0m                                    })[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m                    except Exception as e:[0m
[7m[0m                        logger.warning(f"Image analysis failed for {result.url}: {e}")[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        except ImportError as e:[0m
[7m[0m            logger.warning(f"Multimodal tools not available: {e}")[0m
[7m[0m        except Exception as e:[0m
[7m[0m            logger.error(f"Multimodal analysis failed: {e}")[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        logger.info([0m
[7m[0m            f"Multimodal analysis: {len(multimodal_results['pdf_analyses'])} PDFs, "[0m
[7m[0m            f"{len(multimodal_results['image_analyses'])} images"[0m
[7m[0m        )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        return multimodal_results[0m

[7m[0mdef analyze_pdf_source([0m
[7m[0m    file_path: str,[0m
[7m[0m    query: str,[0m
[7m[0m    extract_tables: bool = True,[0m
[7m[0m    analyze_images: bool = False[0m
[7m[0m) -> Dict[str, Any]:[0m
[7m[0m    """[0m
[7m[0m    Analyze a PDF document for research.[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    Args:[0m
[7m[0m        file_path: Path to PDF file[0m
[7m[0m        query: Research question for context[0m
[7m[0m        extract_tables: Whether to extract tables[0m
[7m[0m        analyze_images: Whether to analyze images in PDF[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    Returns:[0m
[7m[0m        Analysis results with text, tables, and findings[0m
[7m[0m    """[0m
[7m[0m    try:[0m
[7m[0m        from src.tools import get_pdf_parser, get_vision_client[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        parser = get_pdf_parser(use_vision=analyze_images)[0m
[7m[0m        result = parser.parse([0m
[7m[0m            file_path=file_path,[0m
[7m[0m            extract_images=analyze_images,[0m
[7m[0m            extract_tables=extract_tables,[0m
[7m[0m            analyze_images=analyze_images,[0m
[7m[0m            max_pages=30[0m
[7m[0m        )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m        return {[0m
[7m[0m            "file_path": file_path,[0m
[7m[0m            "page_count": result.metadata.page_count,[0m
[7m[0m            "text": result.full_text,[0m
[7m[0m            "tables": [t.model_dump() for p in result.pages for t in p.tables],[0m
[7m[0m            "image_count": result.image_count,[0m
[7m[0m            "metadata": result.metadata.model_dump(),[0m
[7m[0m        }[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    except Exception as e:[0m
[7m[0m        logger.error(f"PDF analysis failed: {e}")[0m
[7m[0m        return {"error": str(e)}[0m

[7m[0m    except Exception as e:[0m

[7m[0m        return {"error": str(e)}[0m

[7m[0mdef analyze_source([0m
[7m[0m    url: str,[0m
[7m[0m    content: str,[0m
[7m[0m    query: str[0m
[7m[0m) -> SourceAnalysis:[0m

[7m[0m

[7m[0m        content: Source content[0m
[7m[0m        query: Research question[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    Returns:[0m
[7m[0m        SourceAnalysis with extracted information[0m
[7m[0m    """[0m
[7m[0m    from src.orchestration.state import create_initial_state[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    state = create_initial_state([0m
[7m[0m        vector_id="standalone",[0m
[7m[0m        query=query,[0m
[7m[0m        application="unknown",[0m
[7m[0m        region="GLOBAL",[0m
[7m[0m        stage=1[0m
[7m[0m    )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    # Create mock search result[0m
[7m[0m    result = SearchResult([0m
[7m[0m        result_id="standalone_001",[0m
[7m[0m        url=url,[0m
[7m[0m        title="Standalone Analysis",[0m
[7m[0m        snippet=content[:500],[0m
[7m[0m        source_type="web",[0m
[7m[0m        domain=url.split("/")[2] if "/" in url else url,[0m
[7m[0m        fetch_status="success",[0m
[7m[0m        content=content,[0m
[7m[0m    )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    state["search_results"] = [result][0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    agent = AnalystAgent()[0m
[7m[0m    result_state = agent.invoke(state)[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    # MED-018, MED-019, MED-020: Default scores from config[0m
[7m[0m    default_confidence = get_threshold("scoring.default_confidence", 0.8)[0m
[7m[0m    default_quality = get_threshold("scoring.default_quality", 0.5)[0m
[7m[0m    default_relevance = get_threshold("scoring.default_relevance", 0.5)[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    # Return first analysis if available[0m
[7m[0m    evidence = result_state.get("evidence_chain", [])[0m
[7m[0m    if evidence:[0m
[7m[0m        ev = evidence[0][0m
[7m[0m        return SourceAnalysis([0m
[7m[0m            source_url=url,[0m
[7m[0m            source_quality=ev.source_quality_score,[0m
[7m[0m            relevance_score=ev.relevance_score,[0m
[7m[0m            entities=[[0m
[7m[0m                ExtractedEntity([0m
[7m[0m                    text=e,[0m
[7m[0m                    entity_type="ORGANIZATION",  # Default[0m
[7m[0m                    confidence=default_confidence,[0m
[7m[0m                    context=""[0m
[7m[0m                )[0m
[7m[0m                for e in ev.entities[0m
[7m[0m            ],[0m
[7m[0m            facts=[[0m
[7m[0m                ExtractedFact([0m
[7m[0m                    fact_text=c,[0m
[7m[0m                    fact_type="factual",[0m
[7m[0m                    confidence=default_confidence,[0m
[7m[0m                    supporting_text=ev.text,[0m
[7m[0m                    entities_involved=[][0m
[7m[0m                )[0m
[7m[0m                for c in ev.claims[0m
[7m[0m            ],[0m
[7m[0m            claims=[],[0m
[7m[0m            key_findings=ev.claims,[0m
[7m[0m            limitations=[][0m
[7m[0m        )[0m
[7m[0m
[7m[0m    return SourceAnalysis([0m
[7m[0m        source_url=url,[0m
[7m[0m        source_quality=default_quality,[0m
[7m[0m        relevance_score=default_relevance,[0m
[7m[0m        entities=[],[0m
[7m[0m        facts=[],[0m
[7m[0m        claims=[],[0m
[7m[0m        key_findings=[],[0m
[7m[0m        limitations=["Analysis failed or no content extracted"][0m
[7m[0m    )[0m

"""Paired-prompt schema for sycophancy + refusal stress tests."""

from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Literal

from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

PromptFraming = Literal["neutral", "leading_positive", "leading_negative", "opposite_frame"]


class PairedPrompt(BaseModel):
    """One paired-prompt set targeting a single underlying factual question.

    Per ELEPHANT methodology, the same factual question is reframed in 4
    ways. A non-sycophantic model returns near-identical factual content
    across all framings (with possibly different surface tone).
    """

    paired_id: str = Field(..., description="Stable id for this paired set.")
    underlying_question: str = Field(..., description="The neutral factual question.")
    expected_factual_anchor: str = Field(
        ...,
        description=(
            "A short text anchor that should appear in any responsible "
            "answer regardless of framing (e.g., '3.4% rise per CMHC')."
        ),
    )
    refusal_acceptable: bool = Field(
        default=False,
        description="If True, refusing all 4 framings is acceptable.",
    )
    prompts: dict[PromptFraming, str] = Field(
        ...,
        description="Map of framing → fully-rendered prompt for that framing.",
    )


class CandidateResponse(BaseModel):
    """A model's response to one framing."""

    framing: PromptFraming
    response_text: str
    refused: bool = False


class PairedPromptResult(BaseModel):
    """All four framings' responses for one paired set."""

    paired_id: str
    responses: list[CandidateResponse]

"""Template registry — loads + validates per-template JSON content."""

from __future__ import annotations

import json
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Literal

from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[3]
TEMPLATES_DIR = REPO_ROOT / "config" / "v6_templates"

SourceTier = Literal["T1", "T2", "T3"]


class FrameDefinition(BaseModel):
    frame_id: str
    frame_name: str


class TemplateContent(BaseModel):
    template_id: str
    template_name: str
    summary: str = Field(..., min_length=20)
    primary_domains: list[str] = Field(..., min_length=1)
    source_tiers: dict[SourceTier, list[str]]
    min_sources_per_tier: dict[SourceTier, int]
    frame_manifest: list[FrameDefinition] = Field(..., min_length=2)
    refusal_patterns: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    sample_questions: list[str] = Field(..., min_length=2)
    out_of_scope_examples: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)


def load_template(template_id: str) -> TemplateContent:
    path = TEMPLATES_DIR / f"{template_id}.json"
    if not path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"Template content not found: {path}")
    payload = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    return TemplateContent.model_validate(payload)


def list_template_ids() -> list[str]:
    if not TEMPLATES_DIR.exists():
        return []
    return sorted(p.stem for p in TEMPLATES_DIR.glob("*.json"))

"""FastAPI app factory for POLARIS v6.

Composes routers, wires OpenTelemetry instrumentation when configured,
and exposes the ASGI app via `app = create_app()` for uvicorn.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import os
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager

from fastapi import Depends, FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware

from polaris_v6 import __version__
from polaris_v6.api.ambiguity import router as ambiguity_router
from polaris_v6.api.auth import (
    require_auth as _require_auth,
    router as auth_router,
    verify_app_startup as _verify_auth_startup,
)
from polaris_v6.api.bundle import router as bundle_router
from polaris_v6.api.charts import router as charts_router
from polaris_v6.api.compare import router as compare_router
from polaris_v6.api.followup import router as followup_router
from polaris_v6.api.health import router as health_router
from polaris_v6.api.memory import router as memory_router
from polaris_v6.api.runs import router as runs_router
from polaris_v6.api.scope import router as scope_router
from polaris_v6.api.stream import router as stream_router
from polaris_v6.api.templates import router as templates_router
from polaris_v6.api.transparency import router as transparency_router
from polaris_v6.api.upload import router as upload_router

# Slice 001 (clinical scope discovery + ambiguity) and slice 002 (clinical
# retrieval). Each lives in polaris_graph.api per slice spec; we mount them
# under /api alongside the v6 routers so the frontend at /intake + /retrieval
# can call them without a separate origin.
from polaris_graph.api.intake_route import router as slice001_intake_router
from polaris_graph.api.retrieval_route import (
    get_fetch_fn as slice002_get_fetch_fn,
    router as slice002_retrieval_router,
)
from polaris_graph.api.generation_route import (
    get_completion_fn as slice003_get_completion_fn,
    router as slice003_generation_router,
)
from polaris_graph.api.audit_bundle_route import (
    get_sign_fn as slice004_get_sign_fn,
    router as slice004_audit_bundle_router,
)
from polaris_graph.api.benchmark_route import (
    get_results_root as slice005_get_results_root,
    router as slice005_benchmark_router,
)
from polaris_graph.api.disambiguation_route import router as disambiguation_router
from polaris_graph.api.graph_route import router as graph_router


@asynccontextmanager
async def _lifespan(_: FastAPI):
    if os.environ.get("OTEL_SEMCONV_STABILITY_OPT_IN"):
        from polaris_v6.observability.otel_init import init_otel

        init_otel()
    yield


def create_app() -> FastAPI:
    # I-carney-004 LAW II: fail-loud at app construction if auth substrate
    # is misconfigured. Skipped via POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED=1 in tests + dev.
    _verify_auth_startup()
    app = FastAPI(
        title="POLARIS",
        version=__version__,
        description="Sovereign Canadian deep research AI",
        lifespan=_lifespan,
        dependencies=[Depends(_require_auth)],
    )
    cors_origins = os.environ.get(
        "POLARIS_V6_CORS_ORIGINS",
        "http://localhost:3000,http://localhost:3737,http://localhost:3738,http://127.0.0.1:3000,http://127.0.0.1:3737,http://127.0.0.1:3738",
    ).split(",")
    app.add_middleware(
        CORSMiddleware,
        allow_origins=[o.strip() for o in cors_origins if o.strip()],
        allow_credentials=False,
        allow_methods=["*"],
        allow_headers=["*"],
    )
    app.include_router(health_router)
    app.include_router(auth_router)
    app.include_router(runs_router)
    app.include_router(stream_router)
    app.include_router(ambiguity_router)
    app.include_router(bundle_router)
    app.include_router(scope_router)
    app.include_router(upload_router)
    app.include_router(charts_router)
    app.include_router(followup_router)
    app.include_router(compare_router)
    app.include_router(memory_router)
    app.include_router(templates_router)
    app.include_router(transparency_router)

    # Slice 001 — POST /api/intake + GET /api/intake/health
    app.include_router(slice001_intake_router, prefix="/api")

    # Slice 002 — POST /api/retrieval + GET /api/retrieval/health.
    # Inject the real Serper + Semantic-Scholar fetcher when keys are
    # present; otherwise leave the dependency at the sentinel default
    # (returns 400 fetch_backend_unavailable, never silently degrades).
    if os.environ.get("SERPER_API_KEY", "").strip():
        from polaris_graph.retrieval2.real_fetcher import build_real_fetcher

        # Build once at startup; fetcher reuses httpx connections per call.
        _real_fetcher = build_real_fetcher()

        def _inject_real_fetcher():
            return _real_fetcher

        app.dependency_overrides[slice002_get_fetch_fn] = _inject_real_fetcher
    app.include_router(slice002_retrieval_router, prefix="/api")

    # Slice 003 — POST /api/generation + GET /api/generation/health.
    # When OPENROUTER_API_KEY is present, inject the real OpenRouter-backed
    # completion_fn (PR 7); otherwise leave the sentinel default in place
    # which returns 400 completion_backend_unavailable per LAW II.
    if os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_API_KEY", "").strip():
        from polaris_graph.generator2.real_completion import build_real_completion

        _real_completion = build_real_completion()

        def _inject_real_completion():
            return _real_completion

        app.dependency_overrides[slice003_get_completion_fn] = _inject_real_completion
    app.include_router(slice003_generation_router, prefix="/api")

    # Slice 004 — POST /api/audit-bundle + GET /api/audit-bundle/health.
    # When POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID is set, build the real GPGSigner and inject
    # it via dep override; otherwise leave sentinel default which yields
    # HTTP 503 (LAW II fail-loud — never ship unsigned bundles).
    if os.environ.get("POLARIS_GPG_KEY_ID", "").strip():
        from polaris_graph.audit_bundle.gpg_signer import build_gpg_signer

        _real_signer = build_gpg_signer()

        def _inject_real_signer():
            return _real_signer.sign

        app.dependency_overrides[slice004_get_sign_fn] = _inject_real_signer
    app.include_router(slice004_audit_bundle_router, prefix="/api")

    # Slice 005 — GET /api/benchmark/{id}/{scoreboard,report,summary}.
    # Reads pre-computed artifacts from POLARIS_BENCHMARK_RESULTS_DIR;
    # operator runs scripts/run_benchmark.py to produce them.
    benchmark_results_dir = os.environ.get(
        "POLARIS_BENCHMARK_RESULTS_DIR", ""
    ).strip()
    if benchmark_results_dir:
        from pathlib import Path as _Path

        _benchmark_root = _Path(benchmark_results_dir)

        def _inject_benchmark_root():
            return _benchmark_root

        app.dependency_overrides[slice005_get_results_root] = (
            _inject_benchmark_root
        )
    app.include_router(slice005_benchmark_router, prefix="/api")

    app.include_router(disambiguation_router, prefix="/api")

    # F-snowball — GET /api/runs/{run_id}/graph (I-snowball-002).
    app.include_router(graph_router, prefix="/api")

    return app


app = create_app()

"""Tests for /templates endpoints."""

from __future__ import annotations

import pytest


@pytest.fixture
def client():
    pytest.importorskip("fastapi")
    from fastapi.testclient import TestClient
    from polaris_v6.api.app import create_app

    return TestClient(create_app())


def test_list_returns_all_templates(client):
    response = client.get("/templates")
    assert response.status_code == 200
    body = response.json()
    ids = {t["template_id"] for t in body}
    assert ids == {
        "clinical",
        "policy",
        "tech",
        "due_diligence",
        "ai_sovereignty",
        "canada_us",
        "workforce",
        "custom",
    }


def test_get_one_returns_full_content(client):
    response = client.get("/templates/policy")
    assert response.status_code == 200
    body = response.json()
    assert body["template_id"] == "policy"
    assert "regulatory_decision" in {f["frame_id"] for f in body["frame_manifest"]}
    assert len(body["sample_questions"]) >= 2


def test_get_unknown_template_404(client):
    response = client.get("/templates/does_not_exist")
    assert response.status_code == 404

"""Test that the sycophancy paired-prompt fixtures load + match the schema.

These fixtures are the dataset that Phase 1 LLM-hookup uses to score
candidate generators against the SycEval CI gate.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import json
from pathlib import Path

import pytest

from polaris_v6.sycophancy.paired_prompts import PairedPrompt

FIXTURE_DIR = Path(__file__).parent / "fixtures" / "sycophancy_v1"


def _load_fixtures() -> dict:
    return json.loads((FIXTURE_DIR / "paired_prompts.json").read_text(encoding="utf-8"))


def test_fixtures_load():
    payload = _load_fixtures()
    assert payload["schema_version"] == "1.0"
    assert len(payload["paired_prompts"]) >= 5


def test_each_paired_prompt_has_four_framings():
    payload = _load_fixtures()
    required = {"neutral", "leading_positive", "leading_negative", "opposite_frame"}
    for paired in payload["paired_prompts"]:
        assert required.issubset(paired["prompts"].keys()), (
            f"{paired['paired_id']} missing framings: {required - paired['prompts'].keys()}"
        )


@pytest.mark.parametrize(
    "paired_id",
    [
        "syc_clinical_001",
        "syc_housing_001",
        "syc_trade_001",
        "syc_defense_001",
        "syc_climate_001",
        "syc_clinical_refuse_001",
        "syc_workforce_001",
        "syc_ai_sov_001",
        "syc_canada_us_001",
        "syc_indigenous_consultation_001",
        "syc_personal_legal_refuse_001",
    ],
)
def test_paired_prompt_validates_against_pydantic(paired_id):
    payload = _load_fixtures()
    matching = [p for p in payload["paired_prompts"] if p["paired_id"] == paired_id]
    assert matching, f"fixture {paired_id} not found"
    paired = PairedPrompt.model_validate(matching[0])
    assert paired.paired_id == paired_id
    assert len(paired.prompts) == 4


def test_refusal_acceptable_marked_correctly():
    payload = _load_fixtures()
    refuse_cases = [p for p in payload["paired_prompts"] if p.get("refusal_acceptable")]
    assert any(
        "stop" in p["underlying_question"].lower()
        or "refuse" in p["paired_id"].lower()
        for p in refuse_cases
    ), "expected at least one refusal-acceptable case to relate to personal advice"


def test_factual_anchors_are_short():
    """Anchors must be short enough that a non-sycophantic model can include verbatim."""
    payload = _load_fixtures()
    for paired in payload["paired_prompts"]:
        if not paired.get("refusal_acceptable"):
            anchor = paired["expected_factual_anchor"]
            assert 3 <= len(anchor.split()) <= 12, (
                f"{paired['paired_id']} anchor wrong length: {anchor!r}"
            )


def test_no_duplicate_paired_ids():
    payload = _load_fixtures()
    ids = [p["paired_id"] for p in payload["paired_prompts"]]
    assert len(ids) == len(set(ids))
